	<script type="pmdelayedscript" data-cfasync="false" data-no-optimize="1" data-no-defer="1" data-no-minify="1">
(function() {
  var slides = document.querySelectorAll('.ct-slide');
  var dots = document.querySelectorAll('.ct-dot');
  var fill = document.getElementById('ct-progress-fill');
  var current = 0;
  var timer;
  var DURATION = 6000;

  function goTo(index) {
    slides[current].classList.remove('ct-active');
    dots[current].classList.remove('ct-dot-active');
    current = index;
    slides[current].classList.add('ct-active');
    dots[current].classList.add('ct-dot-active');
    runProgress();
  }

  function next() {
    goTo((current + 1) % slides.length);
  }

  function runProgress() {
    if (!fill) return;
    fill.style.transition = 'none';
    fill.style.width = '0%';
    clearInterval(timer);
    requestAnimationFrame(function() {
      requestAnimationFrame(function() {
        fill.style.transition = 'width ' + DURATION + 'ms linear';
        fill.style.width = '100%';
      });
    });
    timer = setInterval(next, DURATION);
  }

  dots.forEach(function(dot, i) {
    dot.addEventListener('click', function() { goTo(i); });
  });

  window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
    var nav = document.querySelector('.site-header');
    if (nav) nav.classList.toggle('ct-scrolled', window.scrollY > 60);
  });

  if (slides.length > 0) runProgress();
})();
